SQLite format parser\n//!\n//! Parses SQLite databases containing conversation history stored as JSON blobs.\n//! Designed for state.vscdb-style databases (cursorDiskKV table pattern).\n//!\n//! Plugin config requires:\n//! - `parser.query`: SQL SELECT query (e.g. `SELECT key, value FROM cursorDiskKV`)\n//! - `parser.key_filter`: optional regex to filter on the first column (key)\n//! - `parser.content_path`: optional JSON dot-path within the value blob to reach\n//!   the message array (e.g. `\"messages\"`)\n//! - `parser.role`, `parser.content`, `parser.timestamp`: JSON paths within each\n//!   message object\n//!\n//! Memory notes:\n//! - Opens the DB with SQLITE_OPEN_READ_ONLY — never modifies the source\n//! - Sets `PRAGMA cache_size = -8000` (8 MB page cache)\n//! - Streams rows via rusqlite iterator, never materialises the full table\n\nuse crate::error::{AgentScribeError, Result};\nuse crate::event::{Event, Role};\nuse crate::parser::{extract_field, extract_string, parse_timestamp, ParseContext, SessionInfo};\nuse crate::plugin::{Plugin, SessionDetection, SessionIdSource};\nuse chrono::Utc;\nuse regex::Regex;\nuse rusqlite::{Connection, OpenFlags};\nuse serde_json::Value;\nuse std::path::Path;\n\n/// SQLite parser implementation\npub struct SqliteParser;\n\nimpl SqliteParser {\n    /// Open the database read-only and configure memory limits.\n    fn open_db(path: &Path) -> Result<Connection> {\n        let conn = Connection::open_with_flags(\n            path,\n            OpenFlags::SQLITE_OPEN_READ_ONLY | OpenFlags::SQLITE_OPEN_NO_MUTEX,\n        )\n        .map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n            file: path.display().to_string(),\n            line: None,\n            message: format!(\"cannot open SQLite database: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n\n        // Limit read-cache to 8 MB (negative value → kibibytes)\n        conn.execute_batch(\"PRAGMA cache_size = -8000;\")\n            .map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n                file: path.display().to_string(),\n                line: None,\n                message: format!(\"cannot set PRAGMA cache_size: {}\", e),\n            })?;\n\n        Ok(conn)\n    }\n\n    /// Derive session ID from plugin session-detection config.\n    fn session_id_from_path(source_path: &Path, plugin: &Plugin) -> String {\n        match &plugin.source.session_detection {\n            SessionDetection::OneFilePerSession { session_id_from } => match session_id_from {\n                SessionIdSource::Filename => source_path\n                    .file_stem()\n                    .and_then(|s| s.to_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"unknown\")\n                    .to_string(),\n                SessionIdSource::Field(_) => \"unknown\".to_string(),\n            },\n            _ => \"unknown\".to_string(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Extract a per-key session ID using `key_session_id_regex` (capture group 1).\n    /// Returns `None` if the regex doesn't match.\n    fn extract_key_session_id(re: &Regex, key: &str) -> Option<String> {\n        re.captures(key)\n            .and_then(|c| c.get(1))\n            .map(|m| m.as_str().to_string())\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a JSON value blob from one DB row and return its events.\n    ///\n    /// `row_num` is used for error location only.\n    fn parse_value_blob(\n        key: &str,\n        value_str: &str,\n        context: &ParseContext,\n        plugin: &Plugin,\n        row_num: usize,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<Event>> {\n        // Parse the value as JSON.  If it starts with '{' or '[' it is probably\n        // JSON; otherwise treat it as a plain-text content string.\n        let json: Value = match serde_json::from_str(value_str) {\n            Ok(v) => v,\n            Err(_) => {\n                // Treat the raw string as a single assistant message if we have\n                // no role/content path configured.\n                if plugin.parser.role.is_none() {\n                    let ts = Utc::now();\n                    let mut ev = Event::new(\n                        ts,\n                        context.session_id.clone(),\n                        context.source_agent.clone(),\n                        Role::Assistant,\n                        value_str.to_string(),\n                    );\n                    ev.project = context.project.clone();\n                    ev.model = context.model.clone();\n                    return Ok(vec![ev]);\n                }\n                return Err(AgentScribeError::parse_error_with_line(\n                    &context.source_file,\n                    row_num,\n                    format!(\"cannot parse JSON blob for key '{}': not valid JSON\", key),\n                ));\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Navigate to content_path if configured (e.g. \"messages\" or \"data.turns\").\n        let messages_val: Value = if let Some(ref path) = plugin.parser.content_path {\n            match extract_field(&json, path) {\n                Some(v) => v,\n                None => return Ok(Vec::new()), // path missing in this blob – skip silently\n            }\n        } else {\n            json.clone()\n        };\n\n        // Accept both a JSON array of messages and a single message object.\n        let message_list: Vec<Value> = match messages_val {\n            Value::Array(arr) => arr,\n            Value::Object(_) => vec![messages_val],\n            _ => return Ok(Vec::new()),\n        };\n\n        let mut events = Vec::new();\n        for (msg_idx, msg) in message_list.iter().enumerate() {\n            match Self::parse_message(msg, context, plugin, row_num, msg_idx) {\n                Ok(Some(ev)) => events.push(ev),\n                Ok(None) => {}\n                Err(e) if e.is_skippable() => {\n                    eprintln!(\"Warning: {}\", e);\n                }\n                Err(e) => return Err(e),\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(events)\n    }\n\n    /// Extract a single `Event` from a message object.  Returns `Ok(None)` when\n    /// the message should be silently skipped (unknown role, empty content, etc.).\n    fn parse_message(\n        msg: &Value,\n        context: &ParseContext,\n        plugin: &Plugin,\n        row_num: usize,\n        msg_idx: usize,\n    ) -> Result<Option<Event>> {\n        // Timestamp — fall back to now() if absent or unparseable.\n        let ts = if let Some(ref ts_field) = plugin.parser.timestamp {\n            parse_timestamp(msg, ts_field).unwrap_or_else(|_| Utc::now())\n        } else {\n            Utc::now()\n        };\n\n        // Role is required; skip messages without one.\n        let role_str = match plugin\n            .parser\n            .role\n            .as_ref()\n            .and_then(|f| extract_string(msg, f))\n        {\n            Some(r) => r,\n            None => return Ok(None),\n        };\n\n        let role = if let Some(mapped) = plugin.parser.role_map.get(&role_str) {\n            Role::from_str(mapped).ok_or_else(|| {\n                AgentScribeError::parse_error_with_line(\n                    &context.source_file,\n                    row_num * 10_000 + msg_idx,\n                    format!(\"invalid role_map target: {}\", mapped),\n                )\n            })?\n        } else {\n            match Role::from_str(&role_str) {\n                Some(r) => r,\n                None => return Ok(None), // silently skip unknown roles\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Content — optional; skip empty messages.\n        let content = if let Some(ref content_field) = plugin.parser.content {\n            extract_string(msg, content_field).unwrap_or_default()\n        } else {\n            // No content field configured: serialise the whole message object.\n            msg.to_string()\n        };\n\n        if content.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(None);\n        }\n\n        let mut ev = Event::new(\n            ts,\n            context.session_id.clone(),\n            context.source_agent.clone(),\n            role,\n            content,\n        );\n        ev.project = context.project.clone();\n        ev.model = context.model.clone();\n\n        Ok(Some(ev))\n    }\n}\n\nimpl super::FormatParser for SqliteParser {\n    fn parse(&self, source_path: &Path, plugin: &Plugin) -> Result<Vec<Event>> {\n        let conn = Self::open_db(source_path)?;\n\n        let query_str = plugin.parser.query.as_deref().ok_or_else(|| {\n            AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(\"SQLite format requires query\".into())\n        })?;\n\n        // Compile the key-filter regex once.\n        let key_re: Option<Regex> = plugin\n            .parser\n            .key_filter\n            .as_deref()\n            .map(|pat| {\n                Regex::new(pat).map_err(|e| {\n                    AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(format!(\"invalid key_filter regex: {}\", e))\n                })\n            })\n            .transpose()?;\n\n        // Compile the per-key session-ID regex once.\n        let key_session_re: Option<Regex> = plugin\n            .parser\n            .key_session_id_regex\n            .as_deref()\n            .map(|pat| {\n                Regex::new(pat).map_err(|e| {\n                    AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(format!(\"invalid key_session_id_regex: {}\", e))\n                })\n            })\n            .transpose()?;\n\n        let default_session_id = Self::session_id_from_path(source_path, plugin);\n        let base_context = ParseContext::new(\n            default_session_id.clone(),\n            plugin.plugin.name.clone(),\n            source_path.display().to_string(),\n        );\n\n        let mut stmt = conn\n            .prepare(query_str)\n            .map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n                file: source_path.display().to_string(),\n                line: None,\n                message: format!(\"cannot prepare query: {}\", e),\n            })?;\n\n        let col_count = stmt.column_count();\n\n        let mut rows = stmt.query([]).map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n            file: source_path.display().to_string(),\n            line: None,\n            message: format!(\"cannot execute query: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n\n        let mut events = Vec::new();\n        let mut row_num: usize = 0;\n\n        loop {\n            let row = rows.next().map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n                file: source_path.display().to_string(),\n                line: None,\n                message: format!(\"row read error at row {}: {}\", row_num, e),\n            })?;\n\n            let row = match row {\n                Some(r) => r,\n                None => break,\n            };\n            row_num += 1;\n\n            // Column layout:\n            //   ≥2 columns → col[0] = key, col[1] = value  (cursorDiskKV pattern)\n            //   1 column   → col[0] = value (no key filter applicable)\n            let (key, value_str): (String, String) = if col_count >= 2 {\n                let k: String = row.get::<_, String>(0).unwrap_or_default();\n                let v: String = row.get::<_, String>(1).unwrap_or_default();\n                (k, v)\n            } else {\n                let v: String = row.get::<_, String>(0).unwrap_or_default();\n                (String::new(), v)\n            };\n\n            // Apply key filter.\n            if let Some(ref re) = key_re {\n                if !re.is_match(&key) {\n                    continue;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if value_str.is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Derive per-row session ID from the key when key_session_id_regex is set.\n            let context = if let Some(ref re) = key_session_re {\n                match Self::extract_key_session_id(re, &key) {\n                    Some(sid) => {\n                        let mut ctx = base_context.clone();\n                        ctx.session_id = sid;\n                        ctx\n                    }\n                    None => base_context.clone(),\n                }\n            } else {\n                base_context.clone()\n            };\n\n            match Self::parse_value_blob(&key, &value_str, &context, plugin, row_num) {\n                Ok(mut row_events) => events.append(&mut row_events),\n                Err(e) if e.is_skippable() => {\n                    eprintln!(\"Warning: row {}: {}\", row_num, e);\n                }\n                Err(e) => return Err(e),\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(events)\n    }\n\n    fn detect_sessions(&self, source_path: &Path, plugin: &Plugin) -> Result<Vec<SessionInfo>> {\n        let file_size = std::fs::metadata(source_path)?.len();\n\n        // When key_session_id_regex is set, query the DB to discover distinct\n        // session IDs so the scraper can route events to separate output files.\n        if let Some(ref regex_str) = plugin.parser.key_session_id_regex {\n            let re = Regex::new(regex_str).map_err(|e| {\n                AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(format!(\"invalid key_session_id_regex: {}\", e))\n            })?;\n\n            let key_re: Option<Regex> = plugin\n                .parser\n                .key_filter\n                .as_deref()\n                .map(Regex::new)\n                .transpose()\n                .map_err(|e| {\n                    AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(format!(\"invalid key_filter regex: {}\", e))\n                })?;\n\n            let query_str = plugin.parser.query.as_deref().ok_or_else(|| {\n                AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(\"SQLite format requires query\".into())\n            })?;\n\n            let conn = Self::open_db(source_path)?;\n            let mut stmt = conn\n                .prepare(query_str)\n                .map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n                    file: source_path.display().to_string(),\n                    line: None,\n                    message: format!(\"cannot prepare query: {}\", e),\n                })?;\n\n            let col_count = stmt.column_count();\n            let mut rows = stmt.query([]).map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n                file: source_path.display().to_string(),\n                line: None,\n                message: format!(\"cannot execute query: {}\", e),\n            })?;\n\n            let mut session_ids: Vec<String> = Vec::new();\n            loop {\n                let row = rows.next().map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Parse {\n                    file: source_path.display().to_string(),\n                    line: None,\n                    message: format!(\"row read error: {}\", e),\n                })?;\n                let row = match row {\n                    Some(r) => r,\n                    None => break,\n                };\n\n                let key: String = if col_count >= 2 {\n                    row.get(0).unwrap_or_default()\n                } else {\n                    String::new()\n                };\n\n                if let Some(ref kre) = key_re {\n                    if !kre.is_match(&key) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Some(sid) = Self::extract_key_session_id(&re, &key) {\n                    if !session_ids.contains(&sid) {\n                        session_ids.push(sid);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            if session_ids.is_empty() {\n                // No matching keys — return a single placeholder so the scraper\n                // still marks the file as processed.\n                return Ok(vec![SessionInfo {\n                    session_id: Self::session_id_from_path(source_path, plugin),\n                    start_offset: 0,\n                    end_offset: file_size,\n                    metadata: None,\n                }]);\n            }\n\n            return Ok(session_ids\n                .into_iter()\n                .map(|sid| SessionInfo {\n                    session_id: sid,\n                    start_offset: 0,\n                    end_offset: file_size,\n                    metadata: None,\n                })\n                .collect());\n        }\n\n        // Default: one session per file, ID from filename.\n        let session_id = Self::session_id_from_path(source_path, plugin);\n        Ok(vec![SessionInfo {\n            session_id,\n            start_offset: 0,\n            end_offset: file_size,\n            metadata: None,\n        }])\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use crate::parser::FormatParser;\n    use crate::plugin::{\n        LogFormat, Parser, Plugin, PluginMeta, SessionDetection, SessionIdSource, Source,\n    };\n    use rusqlite::Connection;\n    use std::collections::HashMap;\n    use tempfile::NamedTempFile;\n\n    fn make_plugin(query: &str, content_path: Option<&str>) -> Plugin {\n        Plugin {\n            plugin: PluginMeta {\n                name: \"test-sqlite\".to_string(),\n                version: \"1.0\".to_string(),\n            },\n            source: Source {\n                paths: vec![\"/tmp/test.vscdb\".to_string()],\n                exclude: vec![],\n                format: LogFormat::Sqlite,\n                session_detection: SessionDetection::OneFilePerSession {\n                    session_id_from: SessionIdSource::Filename,\n                },\n                tree: None,\n                truncation_limit: None,\n            },\n            parser: Parser {\n                query: Some(query.to_string()),\n                content_path: content_path.map(String::from),\n                role: Some(\"role\".to_string()),\n                content: Some(\"text\".to_string()),\n                role_map: {\n                    let mut m = HashMap::new();\n                    m.insert(\"AI\".to_string(), \"assistant\".to_string());\n                    m\n                },\n                ..Default::default()\n            },\n            metadata: None,\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn create_test_db(messages_json: &str) -> NamedTempFile {\n        let tmp = NamedTempFile::new().unwrap();\n        let conn = Connection::open(tmp.path()).unwrap();\n        conn.execute_batch(\"CREATE TABLE cursorDiskKV (key TEXT, value TEXT);\")\n            .unwrap();\n        conn.execute(\n            \"INSERT INTO cursorDiskKV (key, value) VALUES (?1, ?2)\",\n            rusqlite::params![\"history.session1\", messages_json],\n        )\n        .unwrap();\n        tmp\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_parse_flat_array() {\n        let blob = r#\"[{\"role\":\"user\",\"text\":\"hello\"},{\"role\":\"assistant\",\"text\":\"hi\"}]\"#;\n        let db = create_test_db(blob);\n        let plugin = make_plugin(\"SELECT key, value FROM cursorDiskKV\", None);\n\n        let parser = SqliteParser;\n        let events = parser.parse(db.path(), &plugin).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(events.len(), 2);\n        assert_eq!(events[0].role, Role::User);\n        assert_eq!(events[0].content, \"hello\");\n        assert_eq!(events[1].role, message\"},{\"type\":\"2\",\"text\":\"assistant message\"}]\"#\n            ],\n        )\n        .unwrap();\n\n        let mut plugin = make_plugin(\"SELECT key, value FROM cursorDiskKV\", None);\n        plugin.parser.key_filter = Some(r\"^bubbleId:\".to_string());\n        plugin.parser.key_session_id_regex = Some(r\"^bubbleId:([^:]+):\".to_string());\n        plugin.parser.role = .parser\n            .role_map\n            .insert(\"1\".to_string(), \"user\".to_string());\n        plugin\n            .parser\n            .role_map\n            .insert(\"2\".to_string(), Role::Assistant);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_detect_sessions_with_no_matching_keys_returns_placeholder() {\n        let tmp = NamedTempFile::new().unwrap();\n        let conn = `lock_exclusive()` call, effectively disabling the timeout.\n30\tfn lock_exclusive_with_timeout(file: &File, timeout: Duration) -> Result<()> {\n31\t    if timeout.is_zero() {\n32\t        // Blocking mode: wait indefinitely (legacy / opt-out behaviour)\n33\t        file.lock_exclusive()?;\n34\t        return Ok(());\n35\t    }\n36\t\n37\t    let start = Instant::now();\n38\t    loop {\n39\t        match file.try_lock_exclusive() {\n40\t            Ok(()) => return Ok(()),\n41\t            Err(e) if e.kind() == std::io::ErrorKind::WouldBlock => {\n42\t                if start.elapsed() >= Scrape state tracking for incremental scraping\n//!\n//! Tracks position per source file for incremental scrapes.\n\nuse crate::error::Result;\nuse crate::event::{ScrapeState, SourceFileState};\nuse chrono::Utc;\nuse fs2::FileExt;\nuse std::fs::{File, OpenOptions};\nuse std::io::{BufReader, BufWriter};\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\nuse std::sync::{Arc, Mutex};\nuse std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n\n/// Default lock timeout (30 seconds).\n#[allow(dead_code)]\nconst DEFAULT_LOCK_TIMEOUT: Duration = Duration::from_secs(30);\n\n/// Poll interval when waiting for the exclusive file lock.\nconst LOCK_POLL_INTERVAL: Duration = Duration::from_millis(50);\n\n/// Acquire an exclusive file lock, retrying until `timeout` elapses.\n///\n/// Uses `try_lock_exclusive()` (non-blocking attempt) in a loop so the caller\n/// never blocks indefinitely.  Returns an error if the lock cannot be obtained\n/// within the allotted time.\n///\n/// When `timeout` is `Duration::ZERO` the function falls back to the blocking\n/// `lock_exclusive()` call, effectively disabling the timeout.\nfn lock_exclusive_with_timeout(file: &File, timeout: Duration) -> Result<()> {\n    if timeout.is_zero() {\n        // Blocking mode: wait indefinitely (legacy / opt-out behaviour)\n        file.lock_exclusive()?;\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    let start = Instant::now();\n    loop {\n        match file.try_lock_exclusive() {\n            Ok(()) => return Ok(()),\n            Err(e) if e.kind() == std::io::ErrorKind::WouldBlock => {\n                if start.elapsed() >= timeout {\n                    return Err(crate::error::AgentScribeError::State(format!(\n                        \"timed out waiting for exclusive lock on state file after {}s\",\n                        timeout.as_secs()\n                    )));\n                }\n                std::thread::sleep(LOCK_POLL_INTERVAL);\n            }\n            Err(e) => return Err(e.into()),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Scrape state manager\npub struct StateManager {\n    state_file: PathBuf,\n    state: Arc<Mutex<ScrapeState>>,\n    /// Maximum time to wait for the exclusive file lock when saving.\n    lock_timeout: Duration,\n}\n\nimpl StateManager {\n    /// Create a new state manager with the default 30-second lock timeout.\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    pub fn new(state_file: PathBuf) -> Result<Self> {\n        Self::new_with_timeout(state_file, DEFAULT_LOCK_TIMEOUT)\n    }\n\n    /// Create a new state manager with a configurable lock timeout.\n    ///\n    /// Pass `Duration::ZERO` to disable the timeout (wait indefinitely).\n    pub fn new_with_timeout(state_file: PathBuf, lock_timeout: Duration) -> Result<Self> {\n        let state = if state_file.exists() {\n            Self::load_state(&state_file)?\n        } else {\n            ScrapeState::new()\n        };\n\n        Ok(StateManager {\n            state_file,\n            state: Arc::new(Mutex::new(state)),\n            lock_timeout,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Load state from file\n    fn load_state(path: &Path) -> Result<ScrapeState> {\n        let file = File::open(path)?;\n\n        // Check if file is empty\n        let metadata = file.metadata()?;\n        if metadata.len() == 0 {\n            return Ok(ScrapeState::new());\n        }\n\n        let reader = BufReader::new(file);\n        let state = serde_json::from_reader(reader).map_err(|e| {\n            crate::error::AgentScribeError::State(format!(\"Failed to parse state: {}\", e))\n        })?;\n        Ok(state)\n    }\n\n    /// Save state to file (with file locking).\n    ///\n    /// The exclusive lock is acquired **before** truncating the file.  This\n    /// prevents a concurrent reader from observing an empty file between the\n    /// truncation and the subsequent write.\n    pub fn save(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        let state = self.state.lock().unwrap();\n        let state_ref = &*state;\n\n        // Ensure parent directory exists\n        if let Some(parent) = self.state_file.parent() {\n            std::fs::create_dir_all(parent)?;\n        }\n\n        // Open WITHOUT O_TRUNC — we must acquire the exclusive lock first so\n        // that no reader can see the file in a truncated-but-not-yet-written\n        // state.\n        let file = OpenOptions::new()\n            .write(true)\n            .create(true)\n            .truncate(false)\n            .open(&self.state_file)?;\n\n        // Acquire the exclusive lock before modifying the file.\n        lock_exclusive_with_timeout(&file, self.lock_timeout)?;\n\n        // Safe to truncate now that we hold the exclusive lock.\n        file.set_len(0)?;\n\n        // File position for a freshly-opened (non-append) file is always 0,\n        // so writing immediately after set_len(0) is correct.\n {}\", e))\n        })?;\n\n        // Lock is released when the file handle inside BufWriter is dropped.\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get state for a file\n    pub fn get_file_state(&self, file_path: &str) -> Option<SourceFileState> {\n        let state = self.state.lock().unwrap();\n        state.sources.get(file_path).cloned()\n    }\n\n    /// Get or create state for a file\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    pub fn get_or_create_file_state(&self, file_path: &str, plugin: &str) -> SourceFileState {\n        let mut state = self.state.lock().unwrap();\n        state\n crate::error::AgentScribeError::FileNotFound(file_path.to_path_buf()))?;\n\n        let metadata = std::fs::metadata(file_path)?;\n        let system_time = metadata.modified()?;\n        // Convert            return Err(AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(\n                        \"JSON tree format requires [source.tree] configuration\".to_string(),\n                    ));\n                }\n            }\n            LogFormat::Sqlite => {\n                if plugin.parser.query.is_none() {\n                    return Err(AgentScribeError::InvalidPlugin(\n                        \"SQLite Pass `0` to\n    /// disable the timeout (wait indefinitely).\n    pub fn new_with_lock_timeout(data_dir: PathBuf, lock_timeout_secs: u64) -> Result<Self> {\n        let plugin_dir = data_dir.join(\"plugins\");\n        let state_file = data_dir.join(\"state\").join(\"scrape-state.json\");\n        let sessions_dir = data_dir.join(\"sessions\");\n\n        // Create directories\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(&plugin_dir)?;\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(&sessions_dir)?;\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(state_file.parent().unwrap())?;\n\n        let plugin_manager = PluginManager::new(plugin_dir);\n        let lock_timeout = Duration::from_secs(lock_timeout_secs);\n        let state_manager = StateManager::new_with_timeout(state_file, lock_timeout)?;\n\n        // Initialize index manager (best-effort — scraping continues without indexing if it fails)\n        let index_manager = match IndexManager::open(&data_dir) {\n            Ok(mgr) => Some(mgr),\n            Err(e) => {\n                eprintln!(\n                    \"Warning: Index not available: {}. Scraping without indexing.\",\n                    e\n                );\n                None\n            }\n        };\n\n        Ok(Scraper {\n            plugin_manager,\n            data_dir,\n            sessions_dir,\n            state_manager,\n            index_manager,\n            index_write_depth: 0,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Load all plugins\n    pub fn load_plugins(&mut self) -> Result<Vec<String>> {\n        self.plugin_manager.load_all()\n    }\n\n    /// Get the plugin manager\n    pub fn plugin_manager(&self) -> &PluginManager {\n        &self.plugin_manager\n    }\n\n    /// Get the plugin manager (mutable)\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    pub fn plugin_manager_mut(&mut self) -> &mut PluginManager {\n        &mut self.plugin_manager\n    }\n\n    /// Get the state manager\n    pub fn state_manager(&self) -> &StateManager {\n        &self.state_manager\n    }\n\n    /// Begin an index write session. Uses depth tracking so nested scrape calls\n    /// (scrape_all → scrape_plugin → scrape_file) only commit at the outermost level.\n    fn begin_index_write(&mut self) {\n        if self.index_write_depth == 0 {\n            if let Some(ref mut mgr) = self.index_manager {\n                if let Err(e) = mgr.begin_write() {\n                    warn!(error = %e, \"failed to open index writer; disabling indexing\");\n                    self.index_manager = None;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        self.index_write_depth += 1;\n    }\n\n    /// End an index write session. Commits and releases the writer only when depth\n    /// returns to zero, making indexed documents visible to concurrent readers.\n    fn end_index_write(&mut self) {\n        if self.index_write_depth > 0 {\n            self.index_write_depth -= 1;\n        }\n        if self.index_write_depth == 0 {\n            if let Some(ref mut mgr) = self.index_manager {\n                if let Err(e) = mgr.finish() {\n                    warn!(error = %e, \"failed to commit index\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Index a session if the index manager is available.\n    /// Returns true if the session was indexed.\n    fn index_session_events(\n        &mut self,\n        events: &[Event],\n        session_id: &str,\n        source_agent: &str,\n        project: Option<&str>,\n        model: Option<&str>,\n    ) -> bool {\n        if let Some(ref mut mgr) = self.index_manager {\n            let manifest =\n                build_manifest_from_events(events, session_id, source_agent, project, model);\n            match mgr.index_session(events, &manifest) {\n                Ok(()) => true,\n                Err(e) => {\n                    warn!(session_id = %session_id, error = %e, \"failed to index session\");\n                    false\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            false\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Discover log files for a plugin\n    pub fn discover_files(&self, plugin: &Plugin) -> Result<Vec<PathBuf>> {\n        let mut files = Vec::new();\n\n        for pattern in &plugin.source.paths {\n            // Expand ~ and environment variables\n            let expanded = shellexpand::full(pattern)\n                .map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Glob(format!(\"Expansion error: {}\", e)))?;\n\n            // Use glob to find matching files\n            let glob_result = glob(&expanded)\n                .map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::Glob(format!(\"Invalid glob: {}\", e)))?;\n\n            for entry in glob_result.filter_map(|e| e.ok()) {\n                let path = entry.as_path();\n\n                // Skip if it matches exclude patterns\n                let mut excluded = false;\n                for exclude_pattern in &plugin.source.exclude {\n                    let exclude_expanded = shellexpand::full(exclude_pattern)\n                        .unwrap_or_default()\n                        .into_owned();\n                    if let Ok(exclude_glob) = glob(&exclude_expanded) {\n                        if exclude_glob.filter_map(|e| e.ok()).any(|p| p == path) {\n                            excluded = true;\n                            break;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if !excluded && path.is_file() {\n                    files.push(path.to_path_buf());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(files)\n    }\n\n    /// Scrape all plugins\n    pub fn scrape_all(&mut self) -> Result<ScrapeResult> {\n        self.begin_index_write();\n\n        let mut total_result = ScrapeResult {\n            sessions_scraped: 0,\n            sessions_indexed: 0,\n            events_written: 0,\n            errors: Vec::new(),\n            files_processed: 0,\n            files_skipped: 0,\n            agent_types: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let plugin_names: Vec<String> = self\n            .plugin_manager\n            .names()\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(String::from)\n            .collect();\n\n        info!(plugins = plugin_names.len(), \"starting scrape_all\");\n\n        for plugin_name in plugin_names {\n            if let Some(plugin) = self.plugin_manager.get(&plugin_name).cloned() {\n                let result = self.scrape_plugin(&plugin)?;\n                total_result.sessions_scraped += result.sessions_scraped;\n                total_result.sessions_indexed += result.sessions_indexed;\n                total_result.events_written += result.events_written;\n                total_result.errors.extend(result.errors);\n                total_result.files_processed += result.files_processed;\n                total_result.files_skipped += result.files_skipped;\n                for agent in result.agent_types {\n                    if !total_result.agent_types.contains(&agent) {\n                        total_result.agent_types.push(agent);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Save updated state\n        self.state_manager.save()?;\n\n        self.end_index_write();\n\n        info!(\n            sessions_scraped = total_result.sessions_scraped,\n            sessions_indexed = total_result.sessions_indexed,\n            \"scrape_all complete\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(total_result)\n    }\n\n    /// Scrape a single plugin\n    pub fn scrape_plugin(&mut self, plugin: &Plugin) -> Result<ScrapeResult> {\n        self.begin_index_write();\n\n        let files = self.discover_files(plugin)?;\n\n        let mut result = ScrapeResult {\n            sessions_scraped: 0,\n            sessions_indexed: 0,\n            events_written: 0,\n            errors: Vec::new(),\n            files_processed: 0,\n            files_skipped: 0,\n            agent_types: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        for file_path in files {\n            let path_str = file_path.to_str().unwrap_or(\"\");\n\n            // Sources with a rolling-window truncation_limit (e.g. Windsurf's 20-conversation\n            // cap) can silently overwrite old conversations without shrinking the file.  Clear\n            // the per-file state before each scrape so we always get a fresh full-read and\n            // never leave stale session files from overwritten conversations.\n            if plugin.source.truncation_limit.is_some() {\n                let _ = self.state_manager.remove_file(path_str);\n            }\n\n            // Check if file needs scraping\n            match self\n                .state_manager\n                .needs_rescrape(&file_path, &plugin.plugin.name)\n            {\n                Ok(true) => {\n                    // Check if truncated (physical file shrink)\n                    let file_state = self.state_manager.get_file_state(path_str);\n                    if let Some(state) = file_state {\n                        let metadata = std::fs::metadata(&file_path)?;\n                        if metadata.len() < state.last_byte_offset {\n                            // File was truncated - remove state and rescan fully\n                            self.state_manager.remove_file(path_str)?;\n                        }\n                    }\n\n                    match self.scrape_file(&file_path, plugin) {\n                        Ok(file_result) => {\n                            result.sessions_scraped += file_result.sessions_scraped;\n                            result.sessions_indexed += file_result.sessions_indexed;\n                            result.events_written += file_result.events_written;\n                            result.errors.extend(file_result.errors);\n                            result.files_processed += 1;\n                        }\n                        Err(e) => {\n                            result.errors.push(ScrapeError {\n                                file: file_path.display().to_string(),\n                                line: None,\n                                message: e.to_string(),\n                            });\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                Ok(false) => {\n                    result.files_skipped += 1;\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    result.errors.push(ScrapeError {\n                        file: file_path.display().to_string(),\n                        line: None,\n                        message: format!(\"State check error: {}\", e),\n                    });\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Populate agent type if any sessions were scraped for this plugin\n        if result.sessions_scraped > 0 {\n            result.agent_types.push(plugin.plugin.name.clone());\n        }\n\n        self.end_index_write();\n\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    /// Scrape a single file\n    pub fn scrape_file(&mut self, file_path: &Path, plugin: &Plugin) -> Result<ScrapeResult> {\n        self.begin_index_write();\n\n        let parser: Box<dyn FormatParser> = match plugin.source.format {\n            LogFormat::Jsonl => Box::new(JsonlParser),\n            LogFormat::Markdown => Box::new(MarkdownParser),\n            LogFormat::JsonTree => Box::new(JsonTreeParser),\n            LogFormat::Sqlite => Box::new(SqliteParser),\n        };\n\n        // Detect sessions in the file\n        let sessions = parser.detect_sessions(file_path, plugin)?;\n\n        // Detect project path for this file\n        let project = self.detect_project(file_path, plugin)?;\n\n        let path_str = file_path.to_str().unwrap_or(\"\");\n\n        let mut result = ScrapeResult {\n            sessions_scraped: 0,\n            sessions_indexed: 0,\n            events_written: 0,\n            errors: Vec::new(),\n            files_processed: 1,\n            files_skipped: 0,\n            agent_types: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        // Parse all events once.  For multi-session files (e.g. Cursor/Windsurf\n        // with key_session_id_regex) each event already carries the correct\n        // session_id set by the parser; we filter below rather than re-parsing\n        // the source for every session.\n        let all_events: Vec<Event> = match parser.parse(file_path, plugin) {\n            Ok(events) => events,\n            Err(e) => {\n                if e.is_skippable() {\n                    result.errors.push(ScrapeError {\n                        file: file_path.display().to_string(),\n                        line: None,\n                        message: e.to_string(),\n                    });\n                    Vec::new()\n                } else {\n                    self.end_index_write();\n                    return Err(e);\n                }\n            }\n        };\n\n        let multi_session = sessions.len() > 1;\n\n        for session_info in sessions {\n            let prefixed_session_id = format!(\"{}/{}\", plugin.plugin.name, session_info.session_id);\n\n            // Detect model for this session\n            let model = self.detect_model(file_path, &session_info, plugin)?;\n\n            // Select events that belong to this session.\n            // For single-session sources every event goes to the one session.\n            // For multi-session sources (key_session_id_regex) filter by session_id.\n            let mut events: Vec<Event> = if multi_session {\n                all_events\n                    .iter()\n                    .filter(|e| e.session_id == session_info.session_id)\n                    .cloned()\n                    .collect()\n            } else {\n                all_events.clone()\n            };\n\n            if events.is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Enrich events with project, model, and file paths\n            for event in &mut events {\n                // Set project\n                if event.project.is_none() {\n                    event.project = project.clone();\n                }\n\n                // Set model\n                if event.model.is_none() {\n                    event.model = model.clone();\n                }\n\n                // Extract file paths\n                if event.file_paths.is_empty() {\n                    event.file_paths = FilePathExtractor::extract_from_event(event, plugin);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Write session to file\n            let session_path = self\n                .sessions_dir\n                .join(&plugin.plugin.name)\n                .join(format!(\"{}.jsonl\", session_info.session_id));\n\n            // Create plugin directory if needed\n            std::fs::create_dir_all(session_path.parent().unwrap())?;\n\n            match Self::write_session(&session_path, &events, plugin) {\n                Ok(_) => {\n                    result.sessions_scraped += 1;\n                    result.events_written += events.len();\n\n                    // Track session in state\n                    self.state_manager\n                        .add_session(path_str, prefixed_session_id.clone())?;\n\n                    if self.index_session_events(\n                        &events,\n                        &prefixed_session_id,\n                        &plugin.plugin.name,\n                        project.as_deref(),\n                        model.as_deref(),\n                    ) {\n                        result.sessions_indexed += 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    result.errors.push(ScrapeError {\n                        file: file_path.display().to_string(),\n                        line: None,\n                        message: format!(\"Write error: {}\", e),\n                    });\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Update file offset state\n        let metadata = std::fs::metadata(file_path)?;\n        self.state_manager.set_offset(path_str, metadata.len())?;\n        self.state_manager.set_modified(path_str, Utc::now())?;\n\n        if result.sessions_scraped > 0 {\n            info!(\n                file = %file_path.display(),\n                sessions_scraped = result.sessions_scraped,\n                sessions_indexed = result.sessions_indexed,\n                \"scrape complete\"\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.end_index_write();\n\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    /// Detect project path for a file\n    fn detect_project(&self, file_path: &Path, plugin: &Plugin) -> Result<Option<String>> {\n        let detection = plugin\n            .parser\n            .project\n            .as_ref()\n            .unwrap_or(&crate::plugin::ProjectDetection::ParentDir);\n\n        match detection {\n            ProjectDetection::ParentDir => {\n                // Get parent directory of the log file\n                if let Some(parent) = file_path.parent() {\n                    Ok(Some(parent.to_string_lossy().to_string()))\n                } else {\n                    Ok(None)\n                }\n            }\n            ProjectDetection::GitRoot => {\n                // Use git rev-parse to find the git root\n                if let Ok(output) = Command::new(\"git\")\n                    .args([\"rev-parse\", \"--show-toplevel\"])\n                    .current_dir(file_path.parent().unwrap_or(file_path))\n                    .output()\n                {\n                    if output.status.success() {\n                        let git_root = String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stdout).trim().to_string();\n                        return Ok(Some(git_root));\n                    }\n                }\n                // Fallback to parent dir\n                if let Some(parent) = file_path.parent() {\n                    Ok(Some(parent.to_string_lossy().to_string()))\n                } else {\n                    Ok(None)\n                }\n            }\n            ProjectDetection::Field { field: _ } => {\n                // For field-based detection, we need to extract from the first event\n                // This is handled in the parser, return None here\n                Ok(None)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Detect model for a session\n    fn detect_model(\n        &self,\n        _file_path: &Path,\n        session_info: &crate::parser::SessionInfo,\n        plugin: &Plugin,\n    ) -> Result<Option<String>> {\n        let detection = plugin\n            .parser\n            .model\n            .as_ref()\n            .unwrap_or(&crate::plugin::ModelDetection::None);\n\n        match detection {\n            ModelDetection::Static { value } => Ok(Some(value.clone())),\n            ModelDetection::None => Ok(None),\n            ModelDetection::Metadata { field } | ModelDetection::Event { field } => {\n                // Try to extract from session metadata\n                if let Some(ref metadata) = session_info.metadata {\n                    if let Some(value) = self.extract_field_recursive(metadata, field) {\n                        if let Some(s) = value.as_str() {\n                            return Ok(Some(s.to_string()));\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n\n                // For metadata files, try to read them\n                if let ModelDetection::Metadata { .. } = detection {\n                    if let Some(ref metadata_config) = plugin.metadata {\n                        let session_id = &session_info.session_id;\n                        let meta_path_str = metadata_config\n                            .session_meta\n                            .as_ref()\n                            .map(|p| p.replace(\"{session_id}\", session_id))\n                            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n                        if !meta_path_str.is_empty() {\n                            let expanded = shellexpand::full(&meta_path_str)\n                                .unwrap_or_default()\n                                .into_owned();\n                            let meta_path = PathBuf::from(expanded.as_str());\n\n                            if meta_path.exists() {\n                                if let Ok(content) = std::fs::read_to_string(&meta_path) {\n                                    if let Ok(json) = serde_json::from_str::<Value>(&content) {\n                                        if let Some(value) =\n                                            self.extract_field_recursive(&json, field)\n                                        {\n                                            if let Some(s) = value.as_str() {\n                                                return Ok(Some(s.to_string()));\n                                            }\n                                        }\n                                    }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n\n                Ok(None)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Extract a field from JSON using dot notation (recursive helper)\n    fn extract_field_recursive(&self, value: &Value, path: &str) -> Option<Value> {\n        let mut current = value;\n        for part in path.split('.') {\n            current = current.get(part)?;\n        }\n        Some(current.clone())\n    }\n\n    /// Write a session to disk\n    fn write_session(path: &Path, events: &[Event], _plugin: &Plugin) -> Result<()> {\n        let file = File::create(path)?;\n        let mut writer = BufWriter::new(file);\n\n        for event in events {\n            let jsonl = event\n                .to_jsonl()\n                .map_err(|e| AgentScribeError::State(format!(\"JSON error: {}\", e)))?;\n            writeln!(writer, \"{}\", jsonl)?;\n        }\n\n        writer.flush()?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get session file path for a session ID\n    pub fn session_path(&self, session_id: &str) -> Option<PathBuf> {\n        // Parse session ID as \"<plugin>/<id>\"\n        let parts: Vec<&str> = session_id.splitn(2, '/').collect();\n        if parts.len() == 2 {\n            let plugin = parts[0];\n            let id = parts[1];\n            Some(self.sessions_dir.join(plugin).join(format!(\"{}.jsonl\", id)))\n        } else {\n            None\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Read a session from disk\n    pub fn read_session(&self, session_id: &str) -> Result<Vec<Event>> {\n        let path = self\n            .session_path(session_id)\n            .ok_or_else(|| AgentScribeError::FileNotFound(PathBuf::from(session_id)))?;\n\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&path)?;\n        let mut events = Vec::new();\n\n        for (line_num, line) in content.lines().enumerate() {\n            if line.trim().is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            match Event::from_jsonl(line) {\n                Ok(event) => events.push(event),\n                Err(e) => {\n                    eprintln!(\"Warning: Invalid JSON at line {}: {}\", line_num + 1, e);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(events)\n    }\n\n    /// List all sessions for a plugin\n    pub fn list_sessions(&self, plugin_name: &str) -> Result<Vec<String>> {\n        let plugin_dir = self.sessions_dir.join(plugin_name);\n\n        if !plugin_dir.exists() {\n            return Ok(Vec::new());\n        }\n\n        let mut sessions = Vec::new();\n\n        for entry in std::fs::read_dir(&plugin_dir)? {\n            let entry = entry?;\n            let path = entry.path();\n\n            if path.extension().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) == Some(\"jsonl\") {\n                if let Some(stem) = path.file_stem().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) {\n                    sessions.push(format!(\"{}/{}\", plugin_name, stem));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(sessions)\n    }\n\n    /// Get all session IDs\n    pub fn all_sessions(&self) -> Result<Vec<String>> {\n        let mut all = Vec::new();\n\n        for plugin_name in self.plugin_manager.names() {\n            all.extend(self.list_sessions(plugin_name)?);\n        }\n\n        Ok(all)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Attempt to git-commit newly scraped sessions.\n///\n/// Called from the CLI after a successful scrape when `[scrape] git_auto_commit = true`.\n/// Silently skips if the data directory is not inside a git repository or nothing new was\n/// scraped. Returns `Ok(true)` when a commit was created, `Ok(false)` when skipped.\npub fn git_auto_commit(data_dir: &Path, result: &ScrapeResult) -> Result<bool> {\n    if result.sessions_scraped == 0 {\n        return Ok(false);\n    }\n\n    // Resolve git root — skip silently if data_dir is not tracked by git.\n    let git_top = Command::new(\"git\")\n        .args([\"rev-parse\", \"--show-toplevel\"])\n        .current_dir(data_dir)\n        .output();\n\n    let git_root = match git_top {\n        Ok(out) if out.status.success() => {\n            PathBuf::from(String::from_utf8_lossy(&out.stdout).trim().to_string())\n        }\n        _ => {\n            debug!(\"git_auto_commit: data_dir is not inside a git repo, skipping\");\n            return Ok(false);\n        }\n    };\n\n    let sessions_dir = data_dir.join(\"sessions\");\n\n    // Stage the sessions directory (use absolute path so it works regardless of cwd).\n    let add_out = Command::new(\"git\")\n        .args([\"add\", sessions_dir.to_str().unwrap_or(\"sessions\")])\n        .current_dir(&git_root)\n        .output()?;\n\n    if !add_out.status.success() {\n        warn!(\n            stderr = %String::from_utf8_lossy(&add_out.stderr),\n            \"git_auto_commit: git add failed\"\n        );\n        return Ok(false);\n    }\n\n    // Build a descriptive commit message.\n    let agents = if result.agent_types.is_empty() {\n        \"unknown\".to_string()\n    } else {\n        result.agent_types.join(\", \")\n    };\n    let msg = format!(\n        \"agentscribe: scraped {} session(s) ({})\",\n        result.sessions_scraped, agents\n    );\n\n    let commit_out = Command::new(\"git\")\n        .args([\"commit\", \"-m\", &msg])\n        .current_dir(&git_root)\n        .output()?;\n\n    if commit_out.status.success() {\n        info!(message = %msg, \"git auto-commit created\");\n        return Ok(true);\n    }\n\n    let stderr = String::from_utf8_lossy(&commit_out.stderr);\n    if stderr.contains(\"nothing to commit\") || stderr.contains(\"nothing added to commit\") {\n        debug!(\"git_auto_commit: nothing new to commit\");\n    } else {\n        warn!(stderr = %stderr, \"git_auto_commit: git commit failed\");\n    }\n    Ok(false)\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use crate::plugin::{\n        LogFormat, Parser, Plugin, PluginMeta, SessionDetection, SessionIdSource, Source,\n    };\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_session_path() {\n        let temp = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let data_dir = temp.path().join(\".agentscribe\");\n        let sessions_dir = data_dir.join(\"sessions\");\n\n        let scraper = Scraper::new(data_dir).unwrap();\n\n        assert_eq!(\n            scraper.session_path(\"test-agent/session-123\"),\n            Some(sessions_dir.join(\"test-agent\").join(\"session-123.jsonl\"))\n        );\n\n        assert_eq!(scraper.session_path(\"invalid\"), None);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_truncation_limit_clears_file_state() {\n        let temp = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let data_dir = temp.path().join(\".agentscribe\");\n\n        // Create a test file\n        let test_file = temp.path().join(\"test.log\");\n        std::fs::write(&test_file, \"test content\").unwrap();\n\n        let mut scraper = Scraper::new(data_dir.clone()).unwrap();\n\n        // Set up initial state for the file\n        let file_path = test_file.to_str().unwrap();\n        scraper\n            .state_manager\n            .add_session(file_path, \"test/session-1\".to_string())\n            .unwrap();\n        scraper.state_manager.set_offset(file_path, 1000).unwrap();\n\n        // Verify state was set\n        let state_before = scraper.state_manager.get_file_state(file_path);\n        assert!(state_before.is_some());\n        assert_eq!(state_before.unwrap().last_byte_offset, 1000);\n\n        // Create a plugin with truncation_limit (like Windsurf)\n        let plugin = Plugin {\n            plugin: PluginMeta {\n                name: \"windsurf\".to_string(),\n                version: \"1.0\".to_string(),\n            },\n            source: Source {\n                paths: vec![test_file.to_str().unwrap().to_string()],\n                exclude: vec![],\n                format: LogFormat::Jsonl,\n                session_detection: SessionDetection::OneFilePerSession {\n                    session_id_from: SessionIdSource::Filename,\n                },\n                tree: Phase 6 made AgentScribe useful to humans reviewing sessions after the fact. Phase 7 makes it useful to agents at task pickup time, and makes individual sessions portable artifacts.\n+\n+### `context` Subcommand — Pre-Task Priming\n+\n+A purpose-built query mode for agent workers. Where `search` is designed for a human typing a keyword, `context` is designed for an agent invoking AgentScribe immediately after claiming a bead — before writing any code.\n+\n+**Interface:**\n+\n+```bash\n+agentscribe context \"<task description>\" [--token-budget <n>] [--project <path>] [--json]\n+```\n+\n+**Behavior:**\n+\n+1. **Search**: runs a relevance-ranked BM25 search against the task description, filtered to `--outcome success --solution-only`, packed to `--token-budget` (default: 3000).\n+2. **Rules**: calls the same extraction pipeline as `agentscribe rules` but outputs inline text rather than writing a file — scoped to `--project` if provided, global otherwise.\n+3. **File knowledge**: parses the task description for file path tokens (anything matching `src/`, `.rs`, `.py`, `.ts`, etc.) and prepends gotchas from `file-knowledge` for each identified file.\n+4. **Output**: a single formatted block, ready for direct prepending into a prompt. Not JSON by default; JSON mode wraps the sections for programmatic assembly.\n+\n+**Output format (default):**\n+\n+```\n+## Prior Context\n+\n+### Past Solutions\n+[packed search results]\n+\n+### Project Conventions\n+[rules extraction, scoped to project]\n+\n+### File Notes\n+[file-knowledge output for files mentioned in task]\n+```\n+\n+**Token budget semantics:** Applied globally across all three sections. Section priority: past solutions > conventions > file notes (most relevant first). If the budget is exhausted before file notes, that section is omitted; if before conventions, both are omitted.\n+\n+**NEEDLE integration:** In `NEEDLE/src/prompt/mod.rs`, the `context_parts` assembly in `build_with_vars` calls `agentscribe context \"<bead_title>\" --token-budget 2000` as a subprocess. Output is added as a fourth context part after skills + learnings. Fire-and-forget: if AgentScribe is not installed or returns empty, `context_parts` is unchanged.\n+\n+**Why `context` and not `search`:** `search` returns raw search result snippets with scores and metadata. `context` returns a structured, injection-ready block. The difference is formatting and composability — a worker calling `context` gets one coherent chunk to prepend; calling `search --json` requires parsing and reassembly.\n+","is_error":false}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"57522d7f-03b7-4972-a9ca-794d51f6bbd3","uuid":"468495df-e81f-41b1-ac7e-9e9c5e81845e","timestamp":"2026-05-01T12:44:00.694Z","tool_use_result":{"stdout":"diff --git a/docs/plan.md b/docs/plan.md\nindex 224eb22..410c00d 100644\n--- a/docs/plan.md\n+++ b/docs/plan.md\n@@ -1027,6 +1027,91 @@ agentscribe digest --since 7d\n \n ---\n \n+## Phase 7: Agent Integration & Session Export\n+\n+Two features that close the loop between AgentScribe's accumulated knowledge and the agents that generate it. Phase 6 made AgentScribe useful to humans reviewing sessions after the fact. Phase 7 makes it useful to agents at task pickup time, and makes individual sessions portable artifacts.\n+\n+### `context` Subcommand — Pre-Task Priming\n+\n+A purpose-built query mode for agent workers. Where `search` is designed for a human typing a keyword, `context` is designed for an agent invoking AgentScribe immediately after claiming a bead — before writing any code.\n+\n+**Interface:**\n+\n+```bash\n+agentscribe context \"<task description>\" [--token-budget <n>] [--project <path>] [--json]\n+```\n+\n+**Behavior:**\n+\n+1. **Search**: runs a relevance-ranked BM25 search against the task description, filtered to `--outcome success --solution-only`, packed to `--token-budget` (default: 3000).\n+2. **Rules**: calls the same extraction pipeline as `agentscribe rules` but outputs inline text rather than writing a file — scoped to `--project` if provided, global otherwise.\n+3. **File knowledge**: parses the task description for file path tokens (anything matching `src/`, `.rs`, `.py`, `.ts`, etc.) and prepends gotchas from `file-knowledge` for each identified file.\n+4. **Output**: a single formatted block, ready for direct prepending into a prompt. Not JSON by default; JSON mode wraps the sections for programmatic assembly.\n+\n+**Output format (default):**\n+\n+```\n+## Prior Context\n+\n+### Past Solutions\n+[packed search results]\n+\n+### Project Conventions\n+[rules extraction, scoped to project]\n+\n+### File Notes\n+[file-knowledge output for files mentioned in task]\n+```\n+\n+**Token budget semantics:** Applied globally across all three sections. Section priority: past solutions > conventions > file notes (most relevant first). If the budget is exhausted before file notes, that section is omitted; if before conventions, both are omitted.\n+\n+**NEEDLE integration:** In `NEEDLE/src/prompt/mod.rs`, the `context_parts` assembly in `build_with_vars` calls `agentscribe context \"<bead_title>\" --token-budget 2000` as a subprocess. Output is added as a fourth context part after skills + learnings. Fire-and-forget: if AgentScribe is not installed or returns empty, `context_parts` is unchanged.\n+\n+**Why `context` and not `search`:** `search` returns raw search result snippets with scores and metadata. `context` returns a structured, injection-ready block. The difference is formatting and composability — a worker calling `context` gets one coherent chunk to prepend; calling `search --json` requires parsing and reassembly.\n+","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
